  • CpxA , the inner-membrane protein , phosphorylates its conserved histidine residue in response to signals and then transphosphorylates the conserved asparate residue in CpxR .2 -- 7 ) Activated CpxR , the phosphorylated form ( pCpxR ) , activates transcription of a set of genes , all of which are involved in envelope protein folding and proteolysis .8 -- 10 ) CpxP , a small periplasmic protein , is thought negatively to regulate CpxA activity by interacting with its periplasmic domain ,5,11,12 ) but CpxP is not required for induction of genes regulated by CpxA/CpxR in the response to envelope stress .13 ) NlpE is an outermembrane lipoprotein that activates the CpxA/CpxR regulon when overexpressed .14 ) Adhesion to hydrophobic surfaces induces the CpxA/CpxR regulon in a NlpE-dependent manner .15 ) CpxR is an OmpR family transcription factor that contains a helix-turn-helix motif at its N-terminus .   • Hall and Silhavy have proposed a model which suggests that OmpR is a positive regulatory factor which activates transcription of both ompF and ompC and that EnvZ is an osmosensor , presumably in the membrane , which somehow modulates the functional state of OmpR to allow the preferential expression of one porin or the other ( 7 ) .   • Introduction The expression of the ompF and ompC porin genes in Escherichia coli is controlled by the response regulatory protein , OmpR , and the histidine kinase sensor protein , EnvZ [ l-4 ] . [7557323]
  • Puriﬁcation and characterization of the OmpR protein , a positive regulator involved in osmoregulatory expression of the ompF and ompC genes in Esch-erichia coli . [11717281]

  • The OmpR protein acts as a positive regulator for expression of both the ompF and ompC genes by binding to the upstream region of their promoters ( Inokuchi et al. 1984 ; Dairi etal . [3010044]
  • It is thus clear that the OmpR protein is the positiveregulator specific for the ompF and ompC genes ( 13-16 ) . [2668281]
